<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:водянистый.html>водяни́стый</a> (15335)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:водянистый.html>водяни́стый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vodjanístyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>watery, watered-down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:водянистый.html>водяни́стый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:картофель.html>карто́фель</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vodjanístyj</b> kartófelʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">watery potatoes</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>watery, wishy-washy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:водянистый.html>водяни́стый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стиль.html>стиль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vodjanístyj</b> stilʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">watery/insipid style</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>pale, watery</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>вода́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vodá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-яно́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-janój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***воевать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:воевать.html>воева́ть</a> (1674)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вой-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voj-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ева́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-evátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, based on the root of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воин.html>во́ин</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vóin</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">soldier</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vojь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">soldier</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:вой.html>во́и</a></i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voi</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">soldiers</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воевать.html>воева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vojevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повоевать.html>повоева́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fight, to war, to wage war, to be at war</li></ol>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> Израиле <a href = vnd.unilang:студент.html>студе́нты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пенсионер.html>пенсионе́ры</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:воевать.html>вою́ют</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:антенна.html>анте́ннами</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сотовый.html>со́товой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:связь.html>свя́зи</a>. </span></li>
</ul></li>

</ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vojevoda</i>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воевода.html>воево́да</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vojevóda</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воевода.html>воево́ды</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воевода.html>воево́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воевода.html>воево́д</a></b>)

***воедино.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:воедино.html>воеди́но</a> (14059)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span>, evidently from <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">въ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">ѥдинъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jedinŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воедино.html>воеди́но</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vojedíno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>together
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собрать.html>собра́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:воедино.html>воеди́но</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sobrátʹ <b>vojedíno</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to collect/bring together</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">odín</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одинокий.html>одино́кий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">odinókij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одиноко.html>одино́ко</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">odinóko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одиночество.html>одино́чество</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">odinóčestvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одиночный.html>одино́чный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">odinóčnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одиночка.html>одино́чка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">odinóčka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:военкомат.html>военкома́т</a> (10752)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Acronym of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:военный.html>вое́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:комиссариат.html>комиссариа́т</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vojénnyj komissariát</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:военкомат.html>военкома́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vojenkomát</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:военкомат.html>военкома́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:военкомат.html>военкома́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:военкомат.html>военкома́тов</a></b>)

***военный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:военный.html>вое́нный</a> (2476)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vojьnьnъ</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vojьna</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">war</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ьnъ</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vojьnъ</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vojь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">soldier</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ьnъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:военный.html>вое́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vojénnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> war; military</li>
<li>martial</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:военный.html>вое́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vojénnyj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:военный.html>вое́нного</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:военный.html>вое́нные</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:военный.html>вое́нных</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>soldier, military man</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вожделе́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voždelétʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to lust, desire strongly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, related to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:желать.html>жела́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">želatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to desire</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***вождь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вождь.html>вождь</a> (1985)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href = vnd.unilang:вождь.html>вождь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voždĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*voďь</i>. Displaced inherited <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">вожь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vožĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вождь.html>вождь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">voždʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вождь.html>вождя́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вождь.html>вожди́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вождь.html>вожде́й</a></b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возбудить.html>возбуди́ть</a> (3694)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">воз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:будить.html>буди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">budítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возбудить.html>возбуди́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozbudítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возбуждать.html>возбужда́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to excite</li>
<li>to arouse, to rouse, to provoke</li>
<li>to stimulate</li>
<li>to incite, to stir up, to instigate</li>
<li>to raise, to bring, to present</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возбуждённый.html>возбуждённый</a> (3694)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возбуждённый.html>возбуждённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozbuždjónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возбудить.html>возбуди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozbudítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возбуждённый.html>возбуждённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozbuždjónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>excited <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">experiencing excitement</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">person, crowd, etc.; normally animate</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>aroused, horny</li>
<li>excited <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">expressing excitement</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">speech, state, etc.; normally inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<tbody><tr>
<th colspan="2" bgcolor="EEF9FF" rowspan="2" style="vertical-align:center;"><a href = vnd.unilang:падеж.html>паде́ж</a></th>

***возбуждать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возбуждать.html>возбужда́ть</a> (9183)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">воз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">буждать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">buždatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, an old form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:будить.html>буди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">budítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to awaken</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">бѹждѫ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">buždǫ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*buditi</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰewdʰ-</i>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">πυνθάνομαι</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">punthánomai</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">बुद्ध</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">buddha</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">bieten</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возбуждать.html>возбужда́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozbuždátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возбудить.html>возбуди́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to excite</li>
<li>to arouse, to rouse, to provoke</li>
<li>to stimulate</li>
<li>to incite, to stir up, to instigate</li>
<li>to raise, to bring, to present</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возбудитель.html>возбуди́тель</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vozbudítelʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возбуждение.html>возбужде́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vozbuždénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возбуждённый.html>возбуждённый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vozbuždjónnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возбуждаться.html>возбужда́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vozbuždátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возбудиться.html>возбуди́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vozbudítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возбуждаться.html>возбужда́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozbuždátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возбудиться.html>возбуди́ться</a></b>)
